      '<li>Drag the highlighted <code>python3</code> from Finder into the list. Toggle it on.</li>' +
      '<li>Repeat the same remove-and-re-add for <strong>Input Monitoring</strong>.</li>' +
      '<li>Quit WillettBot completely (<code>⌘Q</code>) and reopen it.</li>' +
      '</ol>' +
      '<div style="margin-top:12px;display:flex;gap:8px;flex-wrap:wrap">' +
      '<button onclick="revealPythonBinary()" ' +
      'style="background:transparent;color:var(--text2);border:1px solid var(--border2);' +
      'padding:6px 12px;border-radius:6px;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer">Show Python in Finder</button>' +
      '<button onclick="openSystemSettings(\'accessibility\')" ' +
      'style="background:transparent;color:var(--text2);border:1px solid var(--border2);' +
      'padding:6px 12px;border-radius:6px;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer">Open Accessibility</button>' +
      '<button onclick="openSystemSettings(\'inputMonitoring\')" ' +
      'style="background:transparent;color:var(--text2);border:1px solid var(--border2);' +
      'padding:6px 12px;border-radius:6px;font-size:12px;cursor:pointer">Open Input Monitoring</button>' +
      '</div>' +
      '</details>' +
      (pyPath
        ? '<div style="margin-top:12px;font-size:11px;color:var(--text3)">' +
          'Binary path: <code>' + pyPath.replace(/</g, '&lt;') + '</code></div>'
        : '')
    insertCardIntoActiveView(card)
  }

  function openSystemSettings(pane) {
    if (ipcRenderer) ipcRenderer.send('open-system-settings', pane)
  }

  function revealPythonBinary() {
    if (ipcRenderer) ipcRenderer.send('reveal-python-binary')
  }

  // One-click fix for the TCC hash-churn problem. Calls tccutil reset on
  // the main process — no admin password needed for bundle-scoped resets.
  // After this runs, the next click attempt will trigger a fresh macOS
  // permission prompt instead of silently no-opping.
  //
  // Explicitly attached to window.* at the bottom of this file so inline
  // `onclick="resetMacPermissions()"` in dynamically-inserted cards always
  // resolves — some Electron versions fail to bubble non-window closures
  // into inline handlers when the card is added via innerHTML.
  function resetMacPermissions() {
    if (!ipcRenderer) { alert('Electron IPC unavailable — rebuild the app.'); return }
    var btn = document.getElementById('reset-tcc-btn')
    var msg = document.getElementById('reset-tcc-msg')
    if (btn) { btn.disabled = true; btn.textContent = 'Resetting…' }
    if (msg) {
      msg.style.display = 'block'
      msg.style.color = 'var(--text2)'
      msg.textContent = 'Running tccutil reset…'
    }
    ipcRenderer.invoke('reset-tcc').then(function(res) {
      if (msg) {
        msg.style.display = 'block'
        if (res && res.ok) {
          msg.style.color = '#7ee787'
          msg.innerHTML =
            '✓ Done. Now <strong>quit WillettBot (⌘Q)</strong> and reopen it. ' +
            'The next time you press Start, macOS will ask for permission — click ' +
            '<em>Open System Settings</em> on the prompt and toggle it on.'
        } else {
          msg.style.color = '#ff8686'
          msg.textContent = 'Reset failed: ' + ((res && res.error) || 'unknown error') +
            '. Try the manual steps below.'
        }
      }
    }).catch(function(e) {
      if (msg) {
        msg.style.display = 'block'
        msg.style.color = '#ff8686'
        msg.textContent = 'Reset failed: ' + (e && e.message ? e.message : String(e))
      }
    }).then(function() {
      if (btn) { btn.disabled = false; btn.textContent = 'Reset macOS permissions' }
    })
  }
  // Make sure inline onclick="resetMacPermissions()" can always reach it.
  window.resetMacPermissions = resetMacPermissions

  // Generic bottom-center toast. variant: 'success' (default, green) |
  // 'warn' (amber). Auto-dismisses after 2.6s.
  function showToast(msg, variant) {
    var t = document.createElement('div')
    var warn = variant === 'warn'
    t.style.cssText =
      'position:fixed;bottom:24px;left:50%;transform:translateX(-50%);' +
      (warn
        ? 'background:#3a2814;color:#ffd198;border:1px solid #b5792d;'
        : 'background:#14331d;color:#a6f0b8;border:1px solid #4a9c6b;') +
      'padding:10px 18px;border-radius:10px;font-size:13px;font-weight:500;' +
      'z-index:99999;box-shadow:0 8px 24px rgba(0,0,0,.35)'
    t.textContent = msg
    document.body.appendChild(t)
    setTimeout(function() { t.remove() }, 2600)
  }
  // Permission-specific wrapper. Kept as its own function for clarity at
  // call sites; always renders green (matches the original behavior).
  function showPermToast(msg) { showToast(msg) }

  // ── ACTIVITY LOG ──
  var activityLog = []
  function logActivity(name, detail) {
    var now = new Date()
    var time = now.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit' })
    activityLog.unshift({ name: name, detail: detail, time: time })
    renderActivity()
  }

  function renderActivity() {
    var list = document.getElementById('activity-list')
    // activity-list only exists on the hub view. When renderActivity fires
    // from other views (e.g. saveRecordedScript calling logActivity) the list
    // isn't in the DOM — bail gracefully instead of crashing. Same for
    // empty-activity, which gets wiped out the first time we render rows.
    if (!list) return
    if (activityLog.length === 0) {
      var empty = document.getElementById('empty-activity')
      if (empty) empty.style.display = 'block'
      else list.innerHTML =
        '<div class="empty-activity" id="empty-activity">' +
        'No automations run yet — try sending an email above.</div>'
      return
    }
    var rows = activityLog.slice(0, 5).map(function(a) {
      return '<div class="activity-row">' +
        '<div class="activity-dot dot-green"></div>' +
        '<div class="activity-name">' + a.name + '</div>' +
        '<div class="activity-detail">' + a.detail + '</div>' +
        '<div class="activity-time">' + a.time + '</div>' +
        '</div>'
    }).join('')
    list.innerHTML = rows
  }

  // ── AUTO CLICKER ──
  function showClkStatus(msg, success) {
    var el = document.getElementById('clk-status-bar')
    el.style.display = 'block'
    el.className = 'status-bar ' + (success ? 'success' : 'error')
    el.textContent = msg
  }

  function setClkStatusText(text) {
    document.getElementById('clk-status-text').textContent = text
  }

  function setRunning(running) {
    document.getElementById('clk-start').disabled = running
    document.getElementById('clk-stop').disabled  = !running
    setClkStatusText(running ? 'running' : 'idle')
  }

  function capturePosition() {
    var btn = document.getElementById('capture-btn')
    btn.classList.add('counting')
    var seconds = 3
    btn.textContent = 'Move your mouse to target — capturing in ' + seconds + '...'
    console.log('[capture] countdown start')

    var tick = setInterval(function() {
      seconds -= 1
      if (seconds > 0) {
        btn.textContent = 'Move your mouse to target — capturing in ' + seconds + '...'
      } else {
        clearInterval(tick)
        btn.textContent = 'Capturing...'
        if (ipcRenderer) {
          console.log('[capture] sending clicker-get-position IPC')
          ipcRenderer.send('clicker-get-position')
        } else {
          btn.classList.remove('counting')
          btn.textContent = 'Capture position (3s countdown — move your mouse to the target)'
          showClkStatus('IPC not available — run this inside Electron.', false)
        }
      }
    }, 1000)
  }

  function startClicker() {
    var xRaw = document.getElementById('clk-x').value
    var yRaw = document.getElementById('clk-y').value
    var intervalRaw = document.getElementById('clk-interval').value
    var limitRaw = document.getElementById('clk-limit-value').value
    var limitUnit = document.getElementById('clk-limit-unit').value

    var x = parseInt(xRaw, 10)
    var y = parseInt(yRaw, 10)
    var interval = parseFloat(intervalRaw)

    if (isNaN(x) || isNaN(y)) { showClkStatus('Target X/Y must be numbers.', false); return }
    if (isNaN(interval) || interval < 0.01) { showClkStatus('Interval must be at least 0.01 seconds.', false); return }

    // Sanity check — (0,0) is almost never a real target. Nudge the user
    // to capture or type a real position first.
    if (x === 0 && y === 0) {
      showClkStatus('Target is (0, 0). Capture a position or type real coordinates first.', false)
      return
    }

    // Parse the "Stop after" field into maxClicks OR maxDuration.
    var maxClicks = 0, maxDuration = 0
    if (limitRaw !== '') {
      var lv = parseFloat(limitRaw)
      if (!isNaN(lv) && lv > 0) {
        if (limitUnit === 'clicks') maxClicks = Math.floor(lv)
        else if (limitUnit === 'seconds') maxDuration = lv
        else if (limitUnit === 'minutes') maxDuration = lv * 60
      }
    }

    var stopKey = document.getElementById('clk-stopkey').value

    var config = {
      x: x,
      y: y,
      interval: interval,
      button: document.getElementById('clk-button').value,
      doubleClick: document.getElementById('clk-double').checked,
      maxClicks: maxClicks,
      maxDuration: maxDuration,
      stopKey: stopKey
    }

    var stopLabel = {esc:'Esc', 'return':'Return', f9:'F9', f10:'F10', f12:'F12'}[stopKey] || stopKey

    // Build a human-friendly "will stop when..." string for the status bar.
    var limitLabel = 'never (until you press ' + stopLabel + ')'
    if (maxClicks > 0) limitLabel = 'after ' + maxClicks + ' click' + (maxClicks === 1 ? '' : 's')
    else if (maxDuration > 0) {
      limitLabel = maxDuration >= 60
        ? 'after ' + (maxDuration / 60) + ' min'
        : 'after ' + maxDuration + 's'
    }

    document.getElementById('clk-count').textContent = '0'
    document.getElementById('clk-target').textContent = x + ', ' + y
    document.getElementById('clk-stopkey-display').textContent = stopLabel
    setRunning(true)
    showClkStatus('Clicker running — ' + interval + 's interval. Will stop ' + limitLabel + '.', true)

    if (ipcRenderer) {
      ipcRenderer.send('clicker-start', config)
    } else {
      showClkStatus('IPC not available — run this inside Electron.', false)
      setRunning(false)
    }

    logActivity('Auto Clicker', 'Start · (' + x + ',' + y + ') every ' + interval + 's')
  }

  function stopClicker() {
    if (ipcRenderer) ipcRenderer.send('clicker-stop')
    setRunning(false)
    showClkStatus('Stopped.', true)
    logActivity('Auto Clicker', 'Stopped at ' + document.getElementById('clk-count').textContent + ' clicks')
  }

  if (ipcRenderer) {
    ipcRenderer.on('clicker-position', function(event, pos) {
      console.log('[capture] received clicker-position reply:', pos)
      var btn = document.getElementById('capture-btn')
      btn.classList.remove('counting')
      btn.textContent = 'Capture position (3s countdown — move your mouse to the target)'

      if (pos && typeof pos.x === 'number' && typeof pos.y === 'number') {
        var xInput = document.getElementById('clk-x')
        var yInput = document.getElementById('clk-y')
        xInput.value = pos.x
        yInput.value = pos.y
        // Fire change events so any listeners see the update.
        xInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }))
        yInput.dispatchEvent(new Event('input', { bubbles: true }))
        showClkStatus('Captured position ' + pos.x + ', ' + pos.y + '.', true)
      } else {
        var errMsg = pos && pos.error ? pos.error : 'unknown error'
        var raw = pos && pos._debug
          ? ' | stdout: ' + JSON.stringify(pos._debug.stdout || '') +
            ' | stderr: ' + JSON.stringify(pos._debug.stderr || '')
          : ''
        console.error('[capture] failed —', errMsg, pos && pos._debug)
        showClkStatus('Could not capture position: ' + errMsg + raw, false)
      }
    })

    ipcRenderer.on('clicker-tick', function(event, data) {
      if (data && typeof data.count === 'number') {
        document.getElementById('clk-count').textContent = data.count
      }
    })

    ipcRenderer.on('clicker-warning', function(event, data) {
      showClkStatus('⚠️ ' + (data && data.message ? data.message : 'Warning'), false)
    })

    ipcRenderer.on('clicker-done', function(event, data) {
      setRunning(false)
      var reason = data && data.reason ? data.reason : 'finished'
      showClkStatus('Clicker ' + reason + ' after ' + (data && data.count || 0) + ' clicks.', true)
      // The pre-flight accessibility probe was removed from clicker.py — it
      // false-positived on cursor edges and display scaling. Users who
      // actually have a permission problem can click the "Clicks not
      // working? Fix permissions →" link under Start/Stop to get the card.
    })
  }

  // ── HUB → BUILDER LAUNCHER ──
  // When a "favorite" card on the hub is clicked, jump into the builder
  // view and immediately open the variables/schedule modal for that script.
  async function launchScriptFromHub(filename) {
    showView('view-builder')
    // Make sure the scripts cache is populated before we try to look up
    // metadata — the builder view might not have been visited yet.
    if (!_scriptsCache || !_scriptsCache.length) {
      await loadScripts()
    }
    runScript(filename)
  }

  // ── BUILDER: LIST SCRIPTS ──
  // The Auto Clicker isn't a JSON script — it's a dedicated view with live
  // controls. But conceptually it belongs in the "all your automations" list,
  // so we prepend it as a virtual entry whose Run button just navigates to
  // its own view.
  function renderScriptsList(scripts) {
    var list = document.getElementById('scripts-list')
    var clickerEntry =
      '<div class="script-item">' +
        '<div class="script-item-main">' +
          '<div class="script-item-name">Auto Clicker</div>' +
          '<div class="script-item-desc">Automate mouse clicks at any speed and position you choose. Live controls, not a JSON script.</div>' +
          '<div class="script-item-meta">built-in · live controls</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="script-item-actions">' +
          '<button class="modal-btn primary" onclick="showView(\'view-clicker\')">Configure</button>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>'

    if (!scripts || !scripts.length) {
      list.innerHTML = clickerEntry +
        '<div class="empty-activity">No other scripts yet. Drop a .json file into willettbot/scripts/ and refresh.</div>'
      return
    }
    var scriptRows = scripts.map(function(s) {
      var safeName = String(s.name || s.filename).replace(/</g, '&lt;')
      var safeDesc = String(s.description || '').replace(/</g, '&lt;')
      var safeFile = String(s.filename).replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
      // Outline ♡ by default, filled ♥ when favorited. `data-file` lets the
      // click handler know which script without needing a per-row closure.
      var favClass = s.favorite ? 'fav-btn is-fav' : 'fav-btn'
      var favGlyph = s.favorite ? '♥' : '♡'
      var favTitle = s.favorite ? 'Unfavorite' : 'Favorite'
      return '<div class="script-item" data-filename="' + safeFile + '">' +
        '<div class="script-item-main">' +
          '<div class="script-item-name">' + safeName + '</div>' +
          '<div class="script-item-desc">' + safeDesc + '</div>' +
          '<div class="script-item-meta">' + s.filename + ' · ' + (s.actionCount || 0) + ' action' + (s.actionCount === 1 ? '' : 's') + '</div>' +
        '</div>' +
        '<div class="script-item-actions">' +
          '<button class="' + favClass + '" title="' + favTitle + '" ' +
            'aria-label="' + favTitle + '" ' +
            'data-file="' + safeFile + '" ' +
            'onclick="toggleFavorite(event, \'' + safeFile + '\')">' + favGlyph + '</button>' +
          '<button class="modal-btn" onclick="editScript(\'' + safeFile + '\')">Edit</button>' +
          '<button class="modal-btn primary" onclick="runScript(\'' + safeFile + '\')">Run</button>' +
        '</div>' +
      '</div>'
    }).join('')
    list.innerHTML = clickerEntry + scriptRows
  }

  // Pulse + scroll-to the script row that was just saved, so the user sees
  // "it's in the list now" without having to navigate away and back. No-op
  // if the row can't be found (shouldn't happen — loadScripts is awaited
  // before this runs, but we're defensive).
  function highlightSavedScript(filename) {
    if (!filename) return
    var esc = (window.CSS && CSS.escape) ? CSS.escape(filename) : filename.replace(/"/g,'\\"')
    var row = document.querySelector('.script-item[data-filename="' + esc + '"]')
    if (!row) return
    try { row.scrollIntoView({ behavior: 'smooth', block: 'center' }) } catch (e) {}
    // Brief cyan highlight so the user's eye catches which one is new.
    var prev = row.style.boxShadow
    row.style.transition = 'box-shadow 0.4s ease'
    row.style.boxShadow = '0 0 0 2px var(--accent)'
    setTimeout(function() { row.style.boxShadow = prev || '' }, 1800)
  }

  // ── FAVORITES ─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────
  // Flipping the heart is optimistic: we update the button visually before
  // the IPC roundtrip so the click feels instant, then correct if the main
  // process rejects it (e.g. script was deleted out from under us).
  async function toggleFavorite(ev, filename) {
    if (ev && ev.stopPropagation) ev.stopPropagation()
    if (!ipcRenderer || !filename) return
    var btn = ev && ev.currentTarget ? ev.currentTarget : null
    var wasFav = btn ? btn.classList.contains('is-fav') : false
    // Optimistic flip so the click feels instant.
    if (btn) {
      btn.classList.toggle('is-fav')
      btn.textContent = btn.classList.contains('is-fav') ? '♥' : '♡'
    }
    // Keep the cached script's flag in sync so hub re-renders are correct.
    if (Array.isArray(_scriptsCache)) {
      var cached = _scriptsCache.find(function(s) { return s.filename === filename })
      if (cached) cached.favorite = !wasFav
    }
    try {
      var res = await ipcRenderer.invoke('toggle-favorite', { filename: filename })
      if (!res || !res.ok) {
        // Revert optimistic UI.
        if (btn) {
          btn.classList.toggle('is-fav')
          btn.textContent = btn.classList.contains('is-fav') ? '♥' : '♡'
        }
        if (Array.isArray(_scriptsCache)) {
          var c2 = _scriptsCache.find(function(s) { return s.filename === filename })
          if (c2) c2.favorite = wasFav
        }
        appendLog && appendLog('warn', 'Could not favorite: ' + ((res && res.error) || 'unknown'))
        return
      }
      // Refresh the hub favorites strip so the change is visible everywhere.
      renderHubFavorites()
    } catch (e) {
      // Revert on error.
      if (btn) {
        btn.classList.toggle('is-fav')
        btn.textContent = btn.classList.contains('is-fav') ? '♥' : '♡'
      }
    }
  }

  // Cache the most recently loaded scripts so runScript() can look up
  // variables / name / description without another IPC round-trip.
  var _scriptsCache = []

  async function loadScripts() {
    if (!ipcRenderer) {
      document.getElementById('scripts-list').innerHTML =
        '<div class="empty-activity">IPC not available — run inside Electron.</div>'
      return
    }
    try {
      var scripts = await ipcRenderer.invoke('list-scripts')
      if (scripts && scripts.error) {
        document.getElementById('scripts-list').innerHTML =
          '<div class="empty-activity">Error loading scripts: ' + scripts.error + '</div>'
        return
      }
      _scriptsCache = scripts || []
      renderScriptsList(scripts)
      // Keep the hub's favorites strip in sync with any script changes that
      // happened in the builder (delete, rename, save).
      renderHubFavorites()
    } catch (e) {
      document.getElementById('scripts-list').innerHTML =
        '<div class="empty-activity">Error loading scripts: ' + e.message + '</div>'
    }
  }

  // Override showView to refresh scripts + schedules when the builder opens,
  // and refresh the favorites strip when the hub opens so newly favorited
  // scripts show up the instant you navigate back.
  var _origShowView = showView
  showView = function(id) {
    _origShowView(id)
    if (id === 'view-builder') { loadScripts(); loadSchedules() }
    if (id === 'view-hub')     { renderHubFavorites(); maybeShowTutorial() }
  }

  // ── HUB: FAVORITES STRIP ──
  // Pulls the current favorites list + their metadata and renders them as
  // auto-cards at the top of the hub. The strip auto-hides when no scripts
  // are favorited so it doesn't clutter empty installs.
  async function renderHubFavorites() {
    var section = document.getElementById('hub-favorites-section')
    var grid    = document.getElementById('hub-favorites-grid')
    if (!section || !grid || !ipcRenderer) return
    try {
      // Need both the favorites set AND each script's metadata (name,
      // description). list-scripts already includes the favorite flag, so
      // we just filter it — one IPC call, not two.
      var scripts = await ipcRenderer.invoke('list-scripts')
      if (!Array.isArray(scripts)) {
        section.style.display = 'none'
        return
      }
      var favs = scripts.filter(function(s) { return s.favorite })
      if (!favs.length) {
        section.style.display = 'none'
        grid.innerHTML = ''
        return
      }
      grid.innerHTML = favs.map(function(s) {
        var safeName = String(s.name || s.filename).replace(/</g, '&lt;')
        var safeDesc = String(s.description || '').replace(/</g, '&lt;')
        var safeFile = String(s.filename).replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
        // Pick a friendly icon based on action signatures — very rough, but
        // a nice touch vs. a generic "script" emoji for every card.
        var icon = '🧩'
        return '<div class="auto-card" onclick="launchScriptFromHub(\'' + safeFile + '\')">' +
                 '<span class="fav-mark">♥</span>' +
                 '<div class="card-icon">' + icon + '</div>' +
                 '<div class="card-title">' + safeName + '</div>' +
                 '<div class="card-desc">' + (safeDesc || 'Tap to run.') + '</div>' +
               '</div>'
      }).join('')
      section.style.display = 'block'
    } catch (e) {
      // Don't surface an error card on the hub — silently hide.
      section.style.display = 'none'
    }
  }

  // Initial render on page load so favorites appear without needing to
  // navigate away + back. Deferred to allow the IPC bridge to initialize.
  setTimeout(function() { renderHubFavorites() }, 50)

  // ── BUILDER: EDIT A SCRIPT ──
  // Two views of the same script:
  //   Simple  — block flow diagram. Each action is a card with inline-editable
  //             fields; drag to reorder, click ✕ to delete.
  //   Advanced — raw JSON textarea for power users.
  // Switching between modes round-trips through _editingScript, so edits from
  // either side feed back into the other.
  var _editingFilename = null
  var _editingScript   = null        // parsed script object (shared state)
  var _editingMode     = 'simple'
  var _dragSourceIndex = null

  // Per-action-type display metadata for the block flow.
  // icon: short glyph shown in the left badge.
  // klass: color scheme class on the icon badge.
  // title: human-readable action name.
  // fields: list of {key, label, type, opts?} describing editable inputs.
  //   type ∈ 'int' | 'number' | 'text' | 'textarea' | 'select' | 'keys'
  var ACTION_TYPES = {
    click:         { icon: '●',  klass: 'mouse',  title: 'Click',
                     fields: [{key:'x',label:'X',type:'int'},{key:'y',label:'Y',type:'int'},
                              {key:'button',label:'Button',type:'select',opts:['left','right','middle']}] },
    double_click:  { icon: '◉',  klass: 'mouse',  title: 'Double-click',
                     fields: [{key:'x',label:'X',type:'int'},{key:'y',label:'Y',type:'int'},
                              {key:'button',label:'Button',type:'select',opts:['left','right','middle']}] },
    drag:          { icon: '↘',  klass: 'mouse',  title: 'Drag',
                     fields: [{key:'fromX',label:'From X',type:'int'},{key:'fromY',label:'From Y',type:'int'},
                              {key:'toX',label:'To X',type:'int'},{key:'toY',label:'To Y',type:'int'},
                              {key:'button',label:'Button',type:'select',opts:['left','right','middle']},
                              {key:'duration',label:'Duration (s)',type:'number'}] },
    move_to:       { icon: '→',  klass: 'mouse',  title: 'Move mouse',
                     fields: [{key:'x',label:'X',type:'int'},{key:'y',label:'Y',type:'int'},
                              {key:'duration',label:'Duration (s)',type:'number'}] },
    type:          { icon: 'T',  klass: 'kb',     title: 'Type text',
                     fields: [{key:'text',label:'Text',type:'text'},
                              {key:'interval',label:'Interval (s)',type:'number'}] },
    press:         { icon: 'K',  klass: 'kb',     title: 'Press key',
                     fields: [{key:'key',label:'Key',type:'text'}] },
    hotkey:        { icon: '⌘',  klass: 'kb',     title: 'Hotkey',
                     fields: [{key:'keys',label:'Keys (+ separated)',type:'keys'}] },
    wait:          { icon: '⏱',  klass: 'wait',   title: 'Wait',
                     fields: [{key:'seconds',label:'Seconds',type:'number'}] },
    say:           { icon: '✎',  klass: 'say',    title: 'Log message',
                     fields: [{key:'message',label:'Message',type:'text'}] },
    open_app:      { icon: '▣',  klass: 'system', title: 'Open app',
                     fields: [{key:'name',label:'App name',type:'text'}] },
    focus_app:     { icon: '▣',  klass: 'system', title: 'Focus app',
                     fields: [{key:'name',label:'App name',type:'text'}] },
    open_file:     { icon: '▤',  klass: 'system', title: 'Open file',
                     fields: [{key:'path',label:'Path or URL',type:'text'},
                              {key:'app', label:'Open with (optional)',type:'text'},
                              {key:'inPlace',label:'In current Finder window',type:'bool'}] },
    wait_for_app:  { icon: '⌛', klass: 'system', title: 'Wait for app',
                     fields: [{key:'name',label:'App name',type:'text'},
                              {key:'timeout',label:'Timeout (s)',type:'number'}] },
    applescript:   { icon: '{}', klass: 'system', title: 'AppleScript',
                     fields: [{key:'script',label:'Script',type:'textarea'},
                              {key:'storeAs',label:'Store as',type:'text'}] },
    prompt:        { icon: '?',  klass: 'prompt', title: 'Prompt user',
                     fields: [{key:'message',label:'Message',type:'text'},
                              {key:'kind',label:'Kind',type:'select',opts:['confirm','input','secure_input']},
                              {key:'storeAs',label:'Store as',type:'text'}] },
    switch_desktop:{ icon: '⇔',  klass: 'system', title: 'Switch desktop',
                     fields: [{key:'direction',label:'Direction',type:'select',opts:['left','right']},
                              {key:'count',label:'How many',type:'int'}] }
  }

  function _unknownActionMeta(name) {
    return { icon: '•', klass: '', title: name || 'Unknown',
             fields: [] }   // unknown actions show read-only in Simple; edit in Advanced
  }

  // Default values used when a block's type is changed to one that requires
  // different fields. We preserve any old field that also appears in the new
  // type's defaults (so click → double_click keeps x/y/button), then fill in
  // missing required fields. Bridges below handle coordinate-bearing conversions
  // (click↔drag share a point even though the field names differ).
  var ACTION_DEFAULTS = {
    click:        { x: 0, y: 0, button: 'left' },
    double_click: { x: 0, y: 0, button: 'left' },
    drag:         { fromX: 0, fromY: 0, toX: 0, toY: 0, button: 'left', duration: 0.3 },
    move_to:      { x: 0, y: 0, duration: 0.3 },
    type:         { text: '', interval: 0.02 },
    press:        { key: 'enter' },
    hotkey:       { keys: [] },
    wait:         { seconds: 1 },
    say:          { message: '' },
    open_app:     { name: '' },
    focus_app:    { name: '' },
    open_file:    { path: '', app: '', inPlace: false },
    wait_for_app: { name: '', timeout: 30 },
    applescript:  { script: '', storeAs: '' },
    prompt:       { message: '', kind: 'confirm', storeAs: '' },
    switch_desktop: { direction: 'right', count: 1 }
  }

  function _convertAction(oldAction, newType) {
    var defaults = ACTION_DEFAULTS[newType] || {}
    var out = { action: newType }
    // Carry forward any compatible keys; fill defaults for the rest.
    Object.keys(defaults).forEach(function(k) {
      out[k] = (oldAction[k] !== undefined) ? oldAction[k] : defaults[k]
    })
    // Bridge coordinate-bearing actions so a click → drag starts at the click
    // point (instead of 0,0) and a drag → click lands on the drop point.
    var oldHasPoint = (typeof oldAction.x === 'number' && typeof oldAction.y === 'number')
    var oldHasDrag  = (typeof oldAction.toX === 'number' && typeof oldAction.toY === 'number')

    if (oldHasPoint && newType === 'drag' && oldAction.fromX === undefined) {
      out.fromX = oldAction.x; out.fromY = oldAction.y
      if (oldAction.toX === undefined) { out.toX = oldAction.x; out.toY = oldAction.y }
    }
    if (oldHasDrag && (newType === 'click' || newType === 'double_click' || newType === 'move_to')
        && oldAction.x === undefined) {
      out.x = oldAction.toX; out.y = oldAction.toY
    }
    return out
  }

  async function editScript(filename) {
    if (!ipcRenderer) return
    var resp = await ipcRenderer.invoke('read-script', filename)
    if (!resp || !resp.ok) {
      alert('Could not open ' + filename + ': ' + ((resp && resp.error) || 'unknown'))
      return
    }
    _editingFilename = filename
    document.getElementById('edit-script-title').textContent = filename
    clearEditError()

    var parsed = null
    try { parsed = JSON.parse(resp.content) } catch (e) { parsed = null }

    if (parsed && typeof parsed === 'object') {
      if (!Array.isArray(parsed.actions)) parsed.actions = []
      _editingScript = parsed
      document.getElementById('edit-script-textarea').value = JSON.stringify(parsed, null, 2)
      _setEditMode('simple')
    } else {
      // File has invalid JSON — open Advanced so the user can repair it.
      _editingScript = null
      document.getElementById('edit-script-textarea').value = resp.content
      _setEditMode('advanced')
      showEditError('Current file is not valid JSON — fix it here to use Simple mode.')
    }

    document.getElementById('edit-script-modal').style.display = 'flex'
  }

  function cancelEditScript() {
    document.getElementById('edit-script-modal').style.display = 'none'
    _editingFilename = null
    _editingScript = null
    _dragSourceIndex = null
  }

  function showEditError(msg) {
    var e = document.getElementById('edit-script-error')
    e.textContent = msg
    e.style.display = 'block'
  }
  function clearEditError() {
    document.getElementById('edit-script-error').style.display = 'none'
  }

  // Move between Simple and Advanced. Serializes/parses through _editingScript
  // so edits in one view survive the switch to the other.
  function switchEditMode(mode) {
    if (mode === _editingMode) return
    if (mode === 'advanced') {
      // Pull any in-progress name/description changes into state first.
      _captureHeaderInputs()
      if (_editingScript) {
        document.getElementById('edit-script-textarea').value =
          JSON.stringify(_editingScript, null, 2)
      }
      clearEditError()
    } else {
      // Advanced → Simple requires valid JSON. If it doesn't parse, stay put.
      var text = document.getElementById('edit-script-textarea').value
      var parsed
      try {
        parsed = JSON.parse(text)
        if (!parsed || typeof parsed !== 'object') throw new Error('must be a JSON object')
        if (!Array.isArray(parsed.actions)) parsed.actions = []
      } catch (e) {
        showEditError('Invalid JSON — ' + e.message + '. Fix it here before switching.')
        return
      }
      _editingScript = parsed
      clearEditError()
    }
    _setEditMode(mode)
  }

  function _setEditMode(mode) {
    _editingMode = mode
    document.getElementById('edit-pane-simple').style.display   = mode === 'simple'   ? '' : 'none'
    document.getElementById('edit-pane-advanced').style.display = mode === 'advanced' ? '' : 'none'
    document.getElementById('edit-mode-simple').classList.toggle('active',   mode === 'simple')
    document.getElementById('edit-mode-advanced').classList.toggle('active', mode === 'advanced')
    if (mode === 'simple') {
      document.getElementById('edit-script-name').value        = (_editingScript && _editingScript.name)        || ''
      document.getElementById('edit-script-description').value = (_editingScript && _editingScript.description) || ''
      renderBlockFlow()
    }
  }

  function _captureHeaderInputs() {
    if (!_editingScript) return
    _editingScript.name        = document.getElementById('edit-script-name').value
    _editingScript.description = document.getElementById('edit-script-description').value
  }

  // ── BLOCK FLOW RENDERING ──
  function renderBlockFlow() {
    var flow = document.getElementById('edit-block-flow')
    flow.innerHTML = ''
    if (!_editingScript || !_editingScript.actions || !_editingScript.actions.length) {
      var empty = document.createElement('div')
      empty.className = 'block-empty'
      empty.textContent = 'No actions yet. Switch to Advanced to paste JSON, or record a new script from the builder.'
      flow.appendChild(empty)
      return
    }
    _editingScript.actions.forEach(function(action, idx) {
      flow.appendChild(_buildBlock(action, idx))
    })
  }

  function _buildBlock(action, idx) {
    var meta = ACTION_TYPES[action.action] || _unknownActionMeta(action.action)

    var wrap = document.createElement('div')
    wrap.className = 'block-wrap'

    var block = document.createElement('div')
    block.className = 'block'
    block.setAttribute('draggable', 'true')
    block.dataset.index = idx

    // Drag handlers — HTML5 DnD. We store the source index on dragstart and
    // highlight the hovered block (above/below) based on mouse Y so users
    // can see exactly where the drop will land.
    block.addEventListener('dragstart', function(e) {
      _dragSourceIndex = idx
      block.classList.add('dragging')
      try { e.dataTransfer.effectAllowed = 'move'; e.dataTransfer.setData('text/plain', String(idx)) } catch (_) {}
    })
    block.addEventListener('dragend', function() {
      block.classList.remove('dragging')
      document.querySelectorAll('.block.drop-target-above,.block.drop-target-below')
        .forEach(function(el) { el.classList.remove('drop-target-above','drop-target-below') })
    })
    block.addEventListener('dragover', function(e) {
      if (_dragSourceIndex === null || _dragSourceIndex === idx) return
      e.preventDefault()
      var rect = block.getBoundingClientRect()
      var isAbove = (e.clientY - rect.top) < rect.height / 2
      block.classList.toggle('drop-target-above', isAbove)
      block.classList.toggle('drop-target-below', !isAbove)
    })
    block.addEventListener('dragleave', function() {
      block.classList.remove('drop-target-above','drop-target-below')
    })
    block.addEventListener('drop', function(e) {
      e.preventDefault()
      var src = _dragSourceIndex
      _dragSourceIndex = null
      block.classList.remove('drop-target-above','drop-target-below')
      if (src === null || src === idx) return
      var rect = block.getBoundingClientRect()
      var insertBefore = (e.clientY - rect.top) < rect.height / 2
      _moveAction(src, idx, insertBefore)
    })

    // Icon badge
    var icon = document.createElement('div')
    icon.className = 'block-icon' + (meta.klass ? ' ' + meta.klass : '')
    icon.textContent = meta.icon
    block.appendChild(icon)

    // Body: title + field inputs
    var body = document.createElement('div')
    body.className = 'block-body'

    var title = document.createElement('div')
    title.className = 'block-title'
    var num = document.createElement('span')
    num.className = 'block-num'
    num.textContent = (idx + 1) + '.'
    title.appendChild(num)

    // Type selector: changes this action's type in-place. Lists every known
    // action; if the block's current type is unknown it's shown too so it can
    // be "upgraded" to a known type in one click.
    var typeSel = document.createElement('select')
    typeSel.className = 'block-type-select'
    var knownKeys = Object.keys(ACTION_TYPES)
    if (!ACTION_TYPES[action.action] && action.action) {
      var optU = document.createElement('option')
      optU.value = action.action
      optU.textContent = action.action + ' (unknown)'
      typeSel.appendChild(optU)
    }
    knownKeys.forEach(function(k) {
      var o = document.createElement('option')
      o.value = k
      o.textContent = ACTION_TYPES[k].title
      typeSel.appendChild(o)
    })
    typeSel.value = action.action
    // Don't let selecting options start a block drag.
    typeSel.addEventListener('mousedown', function(ev) { ev.stopPropagation() })
    typeSel.draggable = false
    typeSel.addEventListener('change', function() {
      var newType = typeSel.value
      if (newType === action.action) return
      _editingScript.actions[idx] = _convertAction(action, newType)
      renderBlockFlow()   // re-render so the new type's fields appear
    })
    title.appendChild(typeSel)
    body.appendChild(title)

    if (meta.fields.length) {
      var fields = document.createElement('div')
      fields.className = 'block-fields'
      meta.fields.forEach(function(f) {
        fields.appendChild(_buildFieldInput(action, f))
      })
      body.appendChild(fields)
    } else if (!ACTION_TYPES[action.action]) {
      var note = document.createElement('div')
      note.className = 'block-field'
      note.style.color = 'var(--text3)'
      note.textContent = 'Unknown action type — edit in Advanced.'
      body.appendChild(note)
    }

    block.appendChild(body)

    // Right-side tool cluster: duplicate + delete.
    var tools = document.createElement('div')
    tools.className = 'block-tools'

    var dup = document.createElement('button')
    dup.className = 'block-dup'
    dup.type = 'button'
    dup.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Duplicate action')
    dup.setAttribute('title', 'Duplicate')
    dup.textContent = '⧉'
    dup.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
      ev.stopPropagation()
      // Deep-clone so edits to the copy don't mutate the original.
      var copy = JSON.parse(JSON.stringify(_editingScript.actions[idx]))
      _editingScript.actions.splice(idx + 1, 0, copy)
      renderBlockFlow()
    })
    dup.addEventListener('mousedown', function(ev) { ev.stopPropagation() })
    dup.draggable = false
    tools.appendChild(dup)

    var rm = document.createElement('button')
    rm.className = 'block-remove'
    rm.type = 'button'
    rm.setAttribute('aria-label', 'Delete action')
    rm.setAttribute('title', 'Delete')
    rm.textContent = '✕'
    rm.addEventListener('click', function(ev) {
      ev.stopPropagation()
      _editingScript.actions.splice(idx, 1)
      renderBlockFlow()
    })
    rm.addEventListener('mousedown', function(ev) { ev.stopPropagation() })
    rm.draggable = false
    tools.appendChild(rm)

    block.appendChild(tools)

    wrap.appendChild(block)
    return wrap
  }

  function _buildFieldInput(action, f) {
    var span = document.createElement('span')
    span.className = 'block-field'

    var label = document.createElement('label')
    label.textContent = f.label
    span.appendChild(label)

    var input
    if (f.type === 'bool') {
      // Checkbox. `span` is the field wrapper; we swap layout so the label
      // sits AFTER the checkbox (reads more naturally for on/off toggles).
      input = document.createElement('input')
      input.type = 'checkbox'
      input.checked = !!action[f.key]
      input.style.margin = '0 6px 0 0'
      input.style.cursor = 'pointer'
      // Re-order: checkbox first, then label on the right.
      span.removeChild(label)
      span.appendChild(input)
      span.appendChild(label)
      label.style.cursor = 'pointer'
      label.addEventListener('click', function() { input.click() })
      // Guard against drag-to-reorder misfire.
      input.addEventListener('mousedown', function(ev) { ev.stopPropagation() })
      input.draggable = false
      input.addEventListener('change', function() {
        action[f.key] = !!input.checked
      })
      return span
    } else if (f.type === 'select') {
      input = document.createElement('select')
      f.opts.forEach(function(opt) {
        var o = document.createElement('option')
        o.value = opt; o.textContent = opt
        input.appendChild(o)
      })
      input.value = (action[f.key] != null ? String(action[f.key]) : f.opts[0])
    } else if (f.type === 'textarea') {
      input = document.createElement('textarea')
      input.rows = 2
      input.style.minWidth = '240px'
      input.style.fontFamily = "'DM Mono', monospace"
      input.style.fontSize = '12px'
      input.style.padding = '4px 8px'
      input.style.background = '#0a0a0b'
      input.style.border = '1px solid var(--border)'
      input.style.color = 'var(--text)'
      input.style.borderRadius = '6px'
      input.style.resize = 'vertical'
      input.value = action[f.key] != null ? String(action[f.key]) : ''
    } else {
      input = document.createElement('input')
      input.type = (f.type === 'int' || f.type === 'number') ? 'number' : 'text'
      if (f.type === 'int' || f.type === 'number') input.classList.add('num')
      else input.classList.add('text')
      if (f.type === 'number') input.step = 'any'
      if (f.key === 'keys' && Array.isArray(action.keys)) {
        input.value = action.keys.join('+')
      } else {
        input.value = action[f.key] != null ? String(action[f.key]) : ''
      }
    }

    // Prevent drag-from-input from starting a block drag.
    input.addEventListener('mousedown', function(ev) { ev.stopPropagation() })
    input.draggable = false

    var write = function() {
      var v = input.value
      if (f.type === 'int') {
        var n = parseInt(v, 10)
        action[f.key] = isNaN(n) ? 0 : n
      } else if (f.type === 'number') {
        var fv = parseFloat(v)
        action[f.key] = isNaN(fv) ? 0 : fv
      } else if (f.type === 'keys') {
        action[f.key] = v.split('+').map(function(s) { return s.trim() }).filter(Boolean)
      } else {
        action[f.key] = v
      }
    }
    input.addEventListener('input', write)
    input.addEventListener('change', write)

    span.appendChild(input)
    return span
  }

  // Reorder helper: takes the action at src, inserts it at dst (before or
  // after), and re-renders. Adjusts the destination index if src < dst since
  // splicing shifts indices.
  function _moveAction(src, dst, insertBefore) {
    if (!_editingScript || !Array.isArray(_editingScript.actions)) return
    var actions = _editingScript.actions
    if (src < 0 || src >= actions.length) return
    var item = actions.splice(src, 1)[0]
    var target = insertBefore ? dst : dst + 1
    if (src < dst) target-- // account for the shift caused by the splice above
    if (target < 0) target = 0
    if (target > actions.length) target = actions.length
    actions.splice(target, 0, item)
    renderBlockFlow()
  }

  async function saveEditScript() {
    if (!ipcRenderer || !_editingFilename) return
    clearEditError()

    var content
    if (_editingMode === 'advanced') {
      // Advanced → parse textarea, then re-serialize so the file is
      // pretty-printed consistently and we keep _editingScript in sync.
      var text = document.getElementById('edit-script-textarea').value
      try {
        var parsed = JSON.parse(text)
        if (!parsed || typeof parsed !== 'object') throw new Error('must be a JSON object')
        if (!Array.isArray(parsed.actions)) parsed.actions = []
        _editingScript = parsed
        content = JSON.stringify(parsed, null, 2)
      } catch (e) {
        showEditError('Invalid JSON — ' + e.message)
        return
      }
    } else {
      // Simple → pull the name/description from their inputs, then serialize.
      _captureHeaderInputs()
      if (!_editingScript) {
        showEditError('Nothing to save.')
        return
      }
      content = JSON.stringify(_editingScript, null, 2)
    }

    try {
      var res = await ipcRenderer.invoke('write-script', {
        filename: _editingFilename,
        content: content
      })
      if (res && res.ok) {
        appendLog('done', '💾 Saved ' + res.filename)
        document.getElementById('edit-script-modal').style.display = 'none'
        var savedName = res.filename
        _editingFilename = null
        _editingScript = null
        showToast('Saved script ✓')
        await loadScripts()
        highlightSavedScript(savedName)
      } else {
        showEditError((res && res.error) || 'Unknown error.')
      }
    } catch (e) {
      showEditError(e.message)
    }
  }

  async function deleteScriptFromEditor() {
    if (!ipcRenderer || !_editingFilename) return
    if (!confirm('Delete ' + _editingFilename + '? This cannot be undone.')) return
    try {
      var res = await ipcRenderer.invoke('delete-script', _editingFilename)
      if (res && res.ok) {
        appendLog('warn', '🗑 Deleted ' + _editingFilename)
        document.getElementById('edit-script-modal').style.display = 'none'
        _editingFilename = null
        _editingScript = null
        loadScripts()
      } else {
        alert('Could not delete: ' + ((res && res.error) || 'unknown'))
      }
    } catch (e) {
      alert('Delete failed: ' + e.message)
    }
  }

  // ── BUILDER: RUN A SCRIPT ──
  function appendLog(klass, message) {
    var out = document.getElementById('script-output')
    var ts = new Date().toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: '2-digit', minute: '2-digit', second: '2-digit' })
    var safe = String(message).replace(/</g, '&lt;')
    out.innerHTML += '<div class="log-line ' + klass + '"><span class="ts">' + ts + '</span>' + safe + '</div>'
    out.scrollTop = out.scrollHeight
  }

  function clearLog() {
    document.getElementById('script-output').innerHTML = ''
  }

  function runScript(filename) {
    if (!ipcRenderer) return
    // Always open the modal — even a script without variables needs to pick
    // between Run Now / Once / Recurring.
    var meta = null
    for (var i = 0; i < _scriptsCache.length; i++) {
      if (_scriptsCache[i].filename === filename) { meta = _scriptsCache[i]; break }
    }
    var vars = (meta && meta.variables) || {}
    var keys = Object.keys(vars)
    openScriptVarsModal(filename, meta, vars, keys)
  }

  function _startScript(filename, variables) {
    clearLog()
    appendLog('step', '▶ Starting ' + filename)
    // Reassurance: the user always has an escape hatch, even when the script
    // is moving the mouse into other apps and stealing focus.
    appendLog('step', '⎋ Press Esc any time to stop.')
    document.getElementById('script-stop-btn').style.display = 'inline-block'
    var payload = { filename: filename }
    if (variables && typeof variables === 'object') payload.variables = variables
    ipcRenderer.send('run-script', payload)
  }

  // ── BUILDER: VARIABLES-EDIT + SCHEDULE MODAL ──
  var _pendingScript = null           // { filename, keys, meta }
  var _pendingScheduleMode = 'now'    // 'now' | 'once' | 'recurring'

  function openScriptVarsModal(filename, meta, vars, keys) {
    _pendingScript = { filename: filename, keys: keys, meta: meta }
    document.getElementById('script-vars-title').textContent =
      'Before we run: ' + (meta && meta.name ? meta.name : filename)
    document.getElementById('script-vars-body').textContent =
      (meta && meta.description) ? meta.description : 'Review the values, then choose when to run.'

    var fieldsEl = document.getElementById('script-vars-fields')
    fieldsEl.innerHTML = ''
    keys.forEach(function(k) {
      var val = vars[k]
      var isMultiline = typeof val === 'string' && (val.length > 80 || val.indexOf('\n') !== -1)
      var wrap = document.createElement('div')
      wrap.className = 'modal-field'
      wrap.style.marginTop = '10px'
      var label = document.createElement('label')
      label.textContent = k
      label.style.display = 'block'
      label.style.fontSize = '12px'
      label.style.opacity = '0.75'
      label.style.marginBottom = '4px'
      label.style.fontFamily = 'DM Mono, monospace'
      var input
      if (isMultiline) {
        input = document.createElement('textarea')
        input.rows = 4
      } else {
        input = document.createElement('input')
        input.type = 'text'
      }
      input.className = 'modal-input'
      input.id = 'scriptvar-' + k
      input.value = (val === null || val === undefined) ? '' : String(val)
      input.style.width = '100%'
      input.style.marginBottom = '2px'
      wrap.appendChild(label)
      wrap.appendChild(input)
      fieldsEl.appendChild(wrap)
    })

    // Pre-populate sensible defaults into the schedule fields.
    var today = new Date()
    var yyyy = today.getFullYear()
    var mm = String(today.getMonth() + 1).padStart(2, '0')
    var dd = String(today.getDate()).padStart(2, '0')
    var onceDateEl = document.getElementById('sched-once-date')
    if (onceDateEl && !onceDateEl.value) onceDateEl.value = yyyy + '-' + mm + '-' + dd
    var onceTimeEl = document.getElementById('sched-once-time')
    if (onceTimeEl && !onceTimeEl.value) onceTimeEl.value = '09:30'

    setScheduleMode('now')
    document.getElementById('script-vars-modal').style.display = 'flex'
    setTimeout(function() {
      var first = fieldsEl.querySelector('input, textarea')
      if (first) first.focus()
    }, 60)
  }

  function setScheduleMode(mode) {
    _pendingScheduleMode = mode
    // Update tab active state
    var tabs = document.querySelectorAll('#script-vars-modal .mode-tab')
    tabs.forEach(function(t) {
      if (t.dataset.schedmode === mode) t.classList.add('active')
      else t.classList.remove('active')
    })
    // Show/hide panels
    document.getElementById('sched-panel-once').classList.toggle('visible', mode === 'once')
    document.getElementById('sched-panel-recurring').classList.toggle('visible', mode === 'recurring')
    // Update submit button label
    var btn = document.getElementById('script-vars-submit')
    if (btn) {
      if (mode === 'once')      btn.textContent = 'Schedule Once'
      else if (mode === 'recurring') btn.textContent = 'Set Recurring Schedule'
      else                      btn.textContent = 'Run Script'
    }
  }

  function cancelScriptVars() {
    document.getElementById('script-vars-modal').style.display = 'none'
    _pendingScript = null
  }

  async function confirmScriptVars() {
    if (!_pendingScript) return
    var values = {}
    _pendingScript.keys.forEach(function(k) {
      var el = document.getElementById('scriptvar-' + k)
      if (el) values[k] = el.value
    })
    var filename = _pendingScript.filename
    var meta = _pendingScript.meta
    var mode = _pendingScheduleMode

    if (mode === 'now') {
      document.getElementById('script-vars-modal').style.display = 'none'
      _pendingScript = null
      _startScript(filename, values)
      return
    }

    // Build the schedule payload and save it.
    var payload = {
      filename: filename,
      scriptName: (meta && meta.name) || filename,
      variables: values,
      mode: mode
    }
    if (mode === 'once') {
      payload.onceDate = document.getElementById('sched-once-date').value
      payload.onceTime = document.getElementById('sched-once-time').value
      if (!payload.onceDate || !payload.onceTime) {
        alert('Please set both a date and time for a one-time schedule.')
        return
      }
    } else if (mode === 'recurring') {
      payload.recurringDay = document.getElementById('sched-recurring-day').value
      payload.recurringTime = document.getElementById('sched-recurring-time').value
      if (!payload.recurringTime) {
        alert('Please set a time for the recurring schedule.')
        return
      }
    }

    try {
      var res = await ipcRenderer.invoke('save-schedule', payload)
      if (res && res.ok) {
        appendLog('done', '📅 Scheduled ' + (meta && meta.name || filename) + ' — ' + describeSchedule(res.schedule))
        logActivity('Script Builder', 'Scheduled ' + (meta && meta.name || filename))
        document.getElementById('script-vars-modal').style.display = 'none'
        _pendingScript = null
        loadSchedules()
      } else {
        alert('Could not save schedule: ' + ((res && res.error) || 'unknown'))
      }
    } catch (e) {
      alert('Save schedule failed: ' + e.message)
    }
  }

  // ── BUILDER: SCHEDULES LIST ──
  function describeSchedule(sch) {
    if (!sch) return ''
    if (sch.mode === 'once') {
      return 'once on ' + sch.onceDate + ' at ' + sch.onceTime
    }
    if (sch.mode === 'recurring') {
      var day = sch.recurringDay === 'daily'
        ? 'every day'
        : 'every ' + sch.recurringDay.charAt(0).toUpperCase() + sch.recurringDay.slice(1)
      return day + ' at ' + sch.recurringTime
    }
    return ''
  }

  function formatNextRun(ts) {
    if (!ts) return '—'
    var d = new Date(ts)
    var now = new Date()
    var sameDay = d.toDateString() === now.toDateString()
    var time = d.toLocaleTimeString([], { hour: 'numeric', minute: '2-digit' })
    if (sameDay) return 'today at ' + time
    var tomorrow = new Date(now); tomorrow.setDate(tomorrow.getDate() + 1)
    if (d.toDateString() === tomorrow.toDateString()) return 'tomorrow at ' + time
    var datePart = d.toLocaleDateString([], { weekday: 'short', month: 'short', day: 'numeric' })
    return datePart + ' at ' + time
  }

  async function loadSchedules() {
    if (!ipcRenderer) return
    var list = document.getElementById('schedules-list')
    try {
      var items = await ipcRenderer.invoke('list-schedules')
      if (!items || !items.length) {
        list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-activity">No scheduled runs yet. Click Run on any script and pick "Once At…" or "Recurring".</div>'
        return
      }
      list.innerHTML = items.map(function(s) {
        var safeName = String(s.scriptName || s.filename).replace(/</g, '&lt;')
        var safeId = String(s.id).replace(/"/g, '&quot;')
        var nextLabel = s.enabled ? ('Next run: ' + formatNextRun(s.nextRun)) : 'Disabled'
        return '<div class="script-item">' +
          '<div class="script-item-main">' +
            '<div class="script-item-name">' + safeName + '</div>' +
            '<div class="script-item-desc">' + describeSchedule(s) + '</div>' +
            '<div class="script-item-meta">' + nextLabel + '</div>' +
          '</div>' +
          '<div class="script-item-actions">' +
            '<button class="modal-btn" onclick="deleteSchedule(\'' + safeId + '\')">Cancel</button>' +
          '</div>' +
        '</div>'
      }).join('')
    } catch (e) {
      list.innerHTML = '<div class="empty-activity">Error loading schedules: ' + e.message + '</div>'
    }
  }

  async function deleteSchedule(id) {
    if (!ipcRenderer) return
    if (!confirm('Remove this scheduled run?')) return
    try {
      await ipcRenderer.invoke('delete-schedule', id)
      loadSchedules()
    } catch (e) {
      alert('Could not remove schedule: ' + e.message)
    }
  }

  // React to server-side schedule changes (e.g. a schedule just fired).
  if (ipcRenderer) {
    ipcRenderer.on('schedules-changed', function() { loadSchedules() })
  }

  function stopScript() {
    if (ipcRenderer) ipcRenderer.send('stop-script')
    appendLog('warn', '⏹ Stop requested')
    document.getElementById('script-stop-btn').style.display = 'none'
  }

  if (ipcRenderer) {
    ipcRenderer.on('script-event', function(event, evt) {
      if (!evt) return
      if (evt.event === 'script-start') {
        appendLog('step', '▶ ' + evt.name + ' (' + evt.total + ' steps)')
      } else if (evt.event === 'step') {
        appendLog('step', '  ◦ step ' + (evt.index + 1) + ': ' + evt.label)
      } else if (evt.event === 'log') {
        appendLog('log', evt.message)
      } else if (evt.event === 'prompt') {
        openScriptPrompt(evt)
      } else if (evt.event === 'warning') {
        appendLog('warn', '⚠ ' + evt.message)
      } else if (evt.event === 'error') {
        appendLog('error', '✖ ' + (evt.message || 'error'))
        document.getElementById('script-stop-btn').style.display = 'none'
        logActivity('Script Builder', 'Error in script')
      } else if (evt.event === 'failsafe') {
        appendLog('warn', '⏹ Stopped')
        document.getElementById('script-stop-btn').style.display = 'none'
      } else if (evt.event === 'script-done') {
        appendLog('done', '✓ Done')
        document.getElementById('script-stop-btn').style.display = 'none'
        logActivity('Script Builder', 'Ran ' + (evt.name || 'script'))
      } else if (evt.event === 'stopped') {
        appendLog('warn', '⏹ Stopped')
        document.getElementById('script-stop-btn').style.display = 'none'
      }
    })
  }

  // ── BUILDER: PROMPT MODAL ──
  var activePromptId = null
  var activePromptKind = 'confirm'

  function openScriptPrompt(evt) {
    activePromptId = evt.id
    activePromptKind = evt.kind || 'confirm'
    document.getElementById('script-prompt-msg').textContent = evt.message || ''
    var input = document.getElementById('script-prompt-input')
    if (activePromptKind === 'input' || activePromptKind === 'secure_input') {
      input.style.display = 'block'
      input.type = activePromptKind === 'secure_input' ? 'password' : 'text'
      input.value = ''
      setTimeout(function() { input.focus() }, 50)
    } else {
      input.style.display = 'none'
    }
    document.getElementById('script-prompt-kind').textContent = activePromptKind === 'secure_input' ? 'Sensitive input (not stored)' : 'Automation paused'
    document.getElementById('script-prompt-modal').style.display = 'flex'
  }

  function respondToScriptPrompt(cancelled) {
    if (!activePromptId) return
    var payload = { id: activePromptId, cancelled: !!cancelled }
    if (!cancelled && (activePromptKind === 'input' || activePromptKind === 'secure_input')) {
      payload.value = document.getElementById('script-prompt-input').value
    }
    if (ipcRenderer) ipcRenderer.send('script-prompt-response', payload)
    document.getElementById('script-prompt-modal').style.display = 'none'
    activePromptId = null
  }

  // ── BUILDER: RECORD A NEW SCRIPT ──
  // The recorder is a pynput-based Python subprocess that listens for a
  // start hotkey, captures mouse clicks + keyboard until an end hotkey, and
  // returns a compiled runner.py-compatible script. The UI below wires up
  // the start/stop buttons, live counter, and save panel.
  var _recordedScript = null       // the compiled script, after the end hotkey fires

  function setRecordStatus(text, running) {
    document.getElementById('record-status-text').textContent = text
    document.getElementById('record-start-btn').disabled = !!running
    document.getElementById('record-cancel-btn').disabled = !running
    // Live privacy warning visibility mirrors the recording state so users
    // see it at the exact moment they might type a password. Hiding on
    // stop also keeps the post-recording save panel from looking alarming.
    var warn = document.getElementById('record-live-warn')
    if (warn) warn.style.display = running ? 'block' : 'none'
  }

  function describeRecordedAction(a) {
    if (!a) return '—'
    function shortPath(p) {
      // Collapse $HOME to ~ for readable path previews.
      if (!p) return ''
      return String(p).length > 48 ? '…' + String(p).slice(-46) : String(p)
    }
    switch (a.action) {
      case 'click':        return 'click (' + a.x + ',' + a.y + ')'
      case 'double_click': return 'double-click (' + a.x + ',' + a.y + ')'
      case 'drag':         return 'drag (' + a.fromX + ',' + a.fromY + ') → (' + a.toX + ',' + a.toY + ')'
      case 'move_to':      return 'move to (' + a.x + ',' + a.y + ')'
      case 'char':         return 'type "' + a.char + '"'
      case 'type':         return 'type "' + (a.text || '').slice(0, 20) + '"'
      case 'press':        return 'press ' + a.key
      case 'hotkey':       return (a.keys || []).join('+')
      case 'wait':         return 'wait ' + a.seconds + 's'
      // Context-aware semantic events — these replace raw clicks when the
      // recorder notices the user switched apps or opened a folder/file.
      case 'focus_app':    return 'switch to ' + (a.name || '?')
      case 'open_app':     return 'open app ' + (a.name || '?')
      case 'wait_for_app': return 'wait for app ' + (a.name || '?')
      case 'open_file':    return (a.inPlace ? 'navigate to ' : 'open ') + shortPath(a.path)
                                  + (a.app ? ' with ' + a.app : '')
      case 'switch_desktop': return 'swipe ' + (a.direction || 'right')
                                  + (a.count && a.count > 1 ? ' ×' + a.count : '')
      default:             return a.action || '?'
    }
  }

  // 3-2-1 countdown before auto-starting so the user has a moment to stop
  // touching the keyboard/mouse after clicking Start. Cancelable if the
  // user clicks Stop during the countdown.
  var _recordCountdownTimer = null
  var _recordCountdownCancelled = false

  function startRecording() {
    if (!ipcRenderer) return
    var startKey = document.getElementById('record-start-hotkey').value
    var endKey   = document.getElementById('record-end-hotkey').value
    if (startKey === endKey) {
      alert('Start and end hotkeys must be different.')
      return
    }
    var name = document.getElementById('record-name').value.trim() || 'Recorded Script'
    _recordedScript = null
    document.getElementById('record-save-panel').style.display = 'none'
    document.getElementById('record-count').textContent = '0'
    document.getElementById('record-last').textContent = '—'
    _recordCountdownCancelled = false

    // Countdown in the status box so the user knows when to let go of the
    // trackpad. On 0 we spawn the recorder with --auto-start so hotkeys
    // aren't required for it to begin capturing.
    var n = 3
    setRecordStatus('starting in ' + n + '...', true)
    if (_recordCountdownTimer) clearInterval(_recordCountdownTimer)
    _recordCountdownTimer = setInterval(function() {
      if (_recordCountdownCancelled) {
        clearInterval(_recordCountdownTimer); _recordCountdownTimer = null
        setRecordStatus('cancelled', false)
        return
      }
      n -= 1
      if (n > 0) {
        setRecordStatus('starting in ' + n + '...', true)
        return
      }
      clearInterval(_recordCountdownTimer); _recordCountdownTimer = null
      ipcRenderer.send('record-start', {
        startHotkey: startKey,
        endHotkey: endKey,
        name: name,
        description: 'Recorded via the mirroring feature.',
        autoStart: true
      })
    }, 1000)
  }

  // Unified stop handler — works during the countdown (cancels) AND during
  // active recording (SIGTERM → clean compile + save panel). Replaces the
  // old "Cancel" button which didn't make clear it actually compiles+saves.
  function stopRecording() {
    if (!ipcRenderer) return
    // Case 1: user is in the pre-recording countdown. Just cancel it.
    if (_recordCountdownTimer) {
      _recordCountdownCancelled = true
      return
    }
    // Case 2: recorder is running. SIGTERM via main.js triggers a clean
    // finalize inside recorder.py — the 'done' event follows with the
    // compiled script and the save panel opens.
    ipcRenderer.send('record-stop')
    setRecordStatus('stopping...', false)
  }
  // Back-compat: some older inline handlers may still call cancelRecording.
  function cancelRecording() { stopRecording() }

  function slugify(s) {
    return String(s || '').toLowerCase()
      .replace(/[^a-z0-9]+/g, '_')
      .replace(/^_+|_+$/g, '')
      .slice(0, 48) || 'recorded_script'
  }

  if (ipcRenderer) {
    ipcRenderer.on('record-event', function(event, evt) {
      if (!evt) return
      if (evt.event === 'ready') {
        // With auto-start the 'ready' message is fleeting — 'started' arrives
        // right after. Still show something so there's no blank state.
        if (evt.autoStart) {
          setRecordStatus('starting...', true)
        } else {
          setRecordStatus('press ' + String(evt.startHotkey || 'f9').toUpperCase() + ' to begin', true)
        }
      } else if (evt.event === 'started') {
        var endKey = document.getElementById('record-end-hotkey').value
        var label = String(endKey || 'f10').toUpperCase()
        setRecordStatus('recording — click Stop or press ' + label, true)
      } else if (evt.event === 'captured') {
        // If this event replaces a previous click (e.g., double-click merge),
        // keep the counter flat — the total number of actions in the compiled
        // script hasn't increased.
        if (!evt.replacesPrevious) {
          var n = parseInt(document.getElementById('record-count').textContent, 10) || 0
          document.getElementById('record-count').textContent = n + 1
        }
        document.getElementById('record-last').textContent = describeRecordedAction(evt.action)
      } else if (evt.event === 'done') {
        _recordedScript = evt.script
        setRecordStatus('complete', false)
        var actionCount = ((evt.script && evt.script.actions) || []).length
        document.getElementById('record-saved-count').textContent = actionCount
        var nameField = document.getElementById('record-name').value.trim()
        var filenameInput = document.getElementById('record-save-filename')
        filenameInput.value = slugify(nameField)
        document.getElementById('record-save-description').value = ''
        // Clear any stale "already named" message from a previous recording
        // and wire the input so edits dismiss the message as the user types.
        _clearRecordNameMsg()
        filenameInput.oninput = _clearRecordNameMsg
        document.getElementById('record-save-panel').style.display = 'block'
        appendLog('done', '⏹ Recording finished — ' + actionCount + ' actions captured.')
      } else if (evt.event === 'warning') {
        // Non-fatal — recording continues. Usually means macOS hasn't granted
        // Automation permission, so we can't detect app switches / file opens
        // and the user will only see raw click + type steps. Surface it in the
        // log and pop a one-time banner above the recording controls.
        appendLog('warn', '⚠ ' + (evt.message || 'Recorder warning'))
        showRecorderPermBanner(evt.message || 'WillettBot can\'t detect app switches or file opens right now.')
      } else if (evt.event === 'automation_status') {
        // Emitted once on recorder startup by the Automation probe in
        // recorder.py. Tells us whether osascript calls will succeed BEFORE
        // the user records anything — so we can surface a permission banner
        // immediately instead of waiting for the half-broken experience to
        // manifest (clicks recording, but no app-context detection).
        //
        // 'ok'     → just a quiet log line; everything works.
        // 'denied' → macOS returned -1743; user must reset AppleEvents TCC.
        // 'silent' → osascript ran but returned nothing (ghost TCC cache).
        // 'timeout'→ probe is still waiting on the macOS prompt to be clicked.
        // 'error'  → couldn't run /usr/bin/osascript at all.
        var _s = evt.status || 'unknown'
        if (_s === 'ok') {
          appendLog('log', '✓ Automation probe ok — app-context detection active.')
        } else {
          // Build a detailed log line showing raw probe output so we can
          // diagnose from the log on remote users' machines without needing
          // to pull the file from ~/Library/Logs/WillettBot/automation.log.
          var detail = 'Automation probe: ' + _s
          if (evt.returncode !== null && evt.returncode !== undefined) detail += ' | rc=' + evt.returncode
          if (evt.stdout) detail += ' | stdout=' + evt.stdout
          if (evt.stderr) detail += ' | stderr=' + evt.stderr
          appendLog('warn', '⚠ ' + detail)
          if (_s === 'denied' || _s === 'silent' || _s === 'error') {
            showRecorderPermBanner(evt.message ||
              'Automation permission missing — app-context and folder-open detection are off.')
          }
        }
      } else if (evt.event === 'error') {
        setRecordStatus('error', false)
        alert('Recorder error: ' + (evt.message || 'unknown'))
      } else if (evt.event === 'exit') {
        if (!_recordedScript) setRecordStatus('stopped', false)
      }
    })
  }

  // Show a dismissible amber banner at the top of the recorder view when
  // the recorder emits a permission warning. Dedup: if a banner is already
  // visible we keep the existing one rather than stacking.
  function showRecorderPermBanner(msg) {
    var view = document.getElementById('view-record') || document.getElementById('view-builder')
    if (!view) return
    if (document.getElementById('record-perm-banner')) return
    var div = document.createElement('div')
    div.id = 'record-perm-banner'
    div.style.cssText =
      'margin:0 0 16px;padding:12px 16px;background:rgba(240,165,0,0.1);' +
      'border:1px solid rgba(240,165,0,0.35);border-radius:8px;' +
      'color:var(--amber);font-size:12.5px;line-height:1.55;' +
      'display:flex;gap:12px;align-items:flex-start'
    div.innerHTML =
      '<div style="flex:1">' + String(msg).replace(/</g, '&lt;') + '</div>' +
      '<button style="background:transparent;border:1px solid currentColor;color:inherit;padding:4px 10px;border-radius:6px;cursor:pointer;font-size:11px" onclick="this.parentElement.remove()">Dismiss</button>'
    var firstCard = view.querySelector('.form-card')
    if (firstCard) firstCard.parentNode.insertBefore(div, firstCard)
    else view.appendChild(div)
  }

  // Inline "already named" message helpers. Shown right below the filename
  // input so the user sees the collision without a modal popup — and the save
  // is blocked entirely until they rename (no more "oops I overwrote my old
  // script" traps).
  function _showRecordNameMsg(msg) {
    var el = document.getElementById('record-save-name-msg')
    if (!el) return
    el.textContent = msg
    el.style.display = 'block'
  }
  function _clearRecordNameMsg() {
    var el = document.getElementById('record-save-name-msg')
    if (!el) return
    el.textContent = ''
    el.style.display = 'none'
  }

  // Turn "my_folder_opener" → "My Folder Opener" for use as a display name when
  // the user didn't fill in the pre-recording name field. Strips .json if
  // present, replaces _ and - with spaces, then title-cases. Returns '' for
  // obviously-empty input so the caller can fall through to a real default.
  function _prettifyFilename(fn) {
    var s = String(fn || '').replace(/\.json$/i, '').replace(/[_\-]+/g, ' ').trim()
    if (!s) return ''
    return s.replace(/\b\w/g, function(c) { return c.toUpperCase() })
  }

  async function saveRecordedScript() {
    if (!ipcRenderer || !_recordedScript) return
    _clearRecordNameMsg()
    var filenameInput = document.getElementById('record-save-filename')
    var filename = filenameInput.value.trim()
    var desc = document.getElementById('record-save-description').value.trim()
    // Display-name resolution priority:
    //   1. The pre-recording "name" input, if the user filled it.
    //   2. A prettified version of the save-panel FILENAME the user just
    //      typed — this is the common case: people name their script in the
    //      save panel, not the pre-record input, and before this fix those
    //      scripts all saved with display name "Recorded Script".
    //   3. Whatever the recorder compiled (default "Recorded Script").
    var preRecName = document.getElementById('record-name').value.trim()
    var displayName = preRecName
      || _prettifyFilename(filename)
      || _recordedScript.name
    if (!filename) {
      _showRecordNameMsg('Please enter a filename.')
      filenameInput.focus()
      return
    }
    try {
      var res = await ipcRenderer.invoke('save-recorded-script', {
        filename: filename,
        displayName: displayName,
        description: desc || _recordedScript.description,
        script: _recordedScript
        // Note: no `overwrite` flag — duplicates are a hard stop, not a prompt.
      })
      if (res && res.ok) {
        // Do the user-visible stuff FIRST so a downstream null-ref (e.g. in
        // logActivity when the hub list isn't mounted) can't swallow the
        // green toast and make the user think saving failed.
        var savePanel = document.getElementById('record-save-panel')
        if (savePanel) savePanel.style.display = 'none'
        _recordedScript = null
        // Clear the inputs so the next recording starts with empty fields.
        filenameInput.value = ''
        var descEl = document.getElementById('record-save-description')
        if (descEl) descEl.value = ''
        showToast('Saved script: ' + (displayName || res.filename) + ' ✓')
        try { await loadScripts() } catch (e) { console.error('[loadScripts]', e) }
        try { highlightSavedScript(res.filename) } catch (e) {}
        try { appendLog('done', '💾 Saved recording as ' + res.filename) } catch (e) {}
        try { logActivity('Script Builder', 'Recorded ' + res.filename) } catch (e) {}
      } else if (res && res.conflict) {
        // Don't offer overwrite — block until the user picks a new name.
        _showRecordNameMsg('Already named — "' + (res.filename || filename) +
                           '" exists. Rename to save.')
        filenameInput.focus(); filenameInput.select()
      } else {
        _showRecordNameMsg((res && res.error) || 'Could not save.')
      }
    } catch (e) {
      _showRecordNameMsg('Save failed: ' + e.message)
    }
  }

  function discardRecordedScript() {
    _recordedScript = null
    document.getElementById('record-save-panel').style.display = 'none'
    setRecordStatus('idle', false)
  }

  // ── TUTORIAL / ONBOARDING WALKTHROUGH ─────────────────────────────────
  // Modal overlay that introduces the main parts of the app: the two
  // presets (Auto Clicker, Send Gmail), the Script Builder / recording
  // flow, and Favorites. Shown automatically the first time the hub
  // becomes visible. Replayable any time from the "tour" link in the
  // top-right status bar. Remembers "seen" via localStorage so it doesn't
  // nag returning users.
  var WB_TUTORIAL_SEEN_KEY = 'wb_tutorial_seen_v1'

  var WB_TUTORIAL_STEPS = [
    {
      icon: '👋',
      title: 'Welcome to WillettBot',
      body: "WillettBot does the repetitive stuff on your Mac for you — clicking, typing, filling forms, sending emails. If you can do it once, WillettBot can do it a hundred times. Here's a quick tour of what's inside."
    },
    {
      icon: '🖱️',
      title: 'Preset: Auto Clicker',
      body: "Need to click the same spot over and over? Open <b>Auto Clicker</b> from the hub. Pick where to click, how often, and for how long — WillettBot does the clicking for you. Great for games, refreshing pages, or anything with a lot of button-mashing."
    },
    {
      icon: '✉️',
      title: 'Preset: Send Gmail',
      body: "Click <b>Send Gmail</b> on the hub, fill in who it's going to, a subject, and a body. WillettBot opens a new tab in your default browser with the email pre-filled in Gmail — you review it and press the blue Send button (or Cmd+Enter). No passwords, no middlemen, works in Chrome / Safari / Arc / whatever you use."
    },
    {
      icon: '🧱',
      title: 'Script Builder: record your own',
      body: "For anything else, use the <b>Script Builder</b>. Click <b>Record</b>, do the thing once — click the buttons, type the text, open the files, whatever — then press <b>F10</b> to stop. WillettBot saves it as a reusable script you can replay anytime, and you can edit individual steps afterward too."
    },
    {
      icon: '⭐',
      title: 'Favorites',
      body: "Click the <b>heart</b> on any script to pin it to your hub as a one-click shortcut. Great for the two or three scripts you use daily — no hunting through a list."
    },
    {
      icon: '🚀',
      title: "You're ready",
      body: "That's the whole tour. Try clicking <b>Send Gmail</b> on the hub to see an automation in action, or jump into <b>Script Builder</b> and record something. You can replay this tour anytime using the <b>tour</b> link in the top-right. Tell Myles what's broken."
    }
  ]

  var _wbTutorialStep = 0
  var _wbTutorialInjected = false

  function _wbInjectTutorialStyles() {
    if (_wbTutorialInjected) return
    _wbTutorialInjected = true
    var style = document.createElement('style')
    style.textContent = [
      '#wb-tut-overlay {',
      '  position: fixed; inset: 0; z-index: 99998;',
      '  background: rgba(6, 4, 20, 0.78);',
      '  backdrop-filter: blur(4px); -webkit-backdrop-filter: blur(4px);',
      '  display: flex; align-items: center; justify-content: center;',
      '  animation: wbTutFade 0.25s ease-out;',
      '}',
      '@keyframes wbTutFade { from { opacity: 0 } to { opacity: 1 } }',
      '#wb-tut-card {',

      '}',

      '  position: absolute; top: 14px; right: 16px;',
      '  background: none; border: none; color: rgba(245,243,255,0.5);',

      '}',

      '  margin-bottom: 18px;',

      '  width: 7px; height: 7px; border-radius: 50%;',
      '  background: rgba(245,243,255,0.2); transition: all 0.2s;',
      '}',
